msg:My wife and I decided to visit Xi'an for her birthday from November 30th to December 4th, 2023, and we chose to stay at the Grand Hyatt Xi'an during that time. In short, it is an exceptional hotel, offering super delicious breakfast with a wide variety of both Western and Chinese dishes. The staff is incredibly friendly and accommodating. For examples, the gentleman in the front door of the hotel always welcomed us with very beautiful smile, the lady who took care of our room every day, displaying meticulous attention to detail that never failed to surprise us. The employees at the Italian restaurant were exceptionally kind, going above and beyond to provide extraordinary care and respect. When they discovered it was my wife's birthday, they surprised us with a small cake, decorated our table with balloons, and even offered us complimentary cocktails.
Furthermore, the staff in the Lounge went out of their way to help me arrange a surprise birthday cake for my wife. They decorated the table with great care and passion, and even presented her with a thoughtful gift and a postcard, sharing their kind wishes with us. I almost forgot to mention that they also surprised me by offering a birthday cake when I was in my room. So, we ended up with three birthday cakes in one night that gave us the opportunity to share our joy and share a slice of happiness with the incredible staff. These are just some examples of their great team of their staff. Without doubt, I would highly recommend this hotel if you are planning to visit Xi'an.

msg:Grand Hyatt (Xi'an) is cheaper than Hyatt

If the price of Grand Hyatt is over 700 yuan, it is the only one in the city that is outsold by its younger brother Hyatt [laughing and crying]
The location is indeed a bit remote. The high-tech zone is still a bit far from the city, and it is not close to the scenic spots. From this point of view, it is understandable that the price is inverted with its younger brother.
The quality of all aspects is very online. The first-line brand is still trustworthy. The hardware facilities are well maintained. It doesn't look like a hotel that has been in use for six years. I won't say much about the service and hygiene, which are in line with the level of this price and brand [strong][strong][strong]
The hotel has a strong sense of design. Although the overall color scheme does not use red in a large area, the touch of crimson dotted in the details just highlights the brand's main color‚òûGrand Hyatt red. The lobby is not big, but the irregular glass skylight, special-shaped polyhedron lamps and white curved ***** decorations make it look very sci-fi and futuristic [proud] The gym and swimming pool are all available, and the scale is smaller than expected. The equipment and environment are very good. What surprised me was that there were seven or eight people exercising in the gym at 8 o'clock in the evening, which is rare [snickering] There are five restaurants in the hotel, including Chinese and Western food, buffet, and bar, which can meet all kinds of needs, but the overall quality is not outstanding, much inferior to W [shut up]
The room layout is quite alternative (standard room), with the aisle in the middle and double beds on both sides, probably considering the consideration of privacy. The indoor area is relatively large in the same level, but most of the space is given to the washing area, two independent washbasins, a separate bathroom with a sink, a shower room and a bathtub, and a dedicated separate cloakroom and ironing area [covering face] The TV is squeezed in a small corner on the side, which is quite unique [proud]
Although the layout of the room is not ordinary, the overall aesthetics are still online. The lines, colors, and decorations are integrated with many Chinese elements, and they can easily walk between classic and modern. All hardware facilities are top-notch, electric curtains, smart speakers, and electric switches are all available. The sanitary ware is Grohe, and even the room card is made of wood [laughing and crying]
However, there are some points. The disposable items are too confusing, there are slippers without brand logos, relatively inferior toothbrushes and combs, large bottles of shower gel and shampoo, and even razors are not provided. Drinking water is to save trouble and go directly to Nongfu Spring [picking nose]

The hidden toilet, spacious bathtub, and oversized ceiling spray greatly enhance the happiness of living. The breakfast category is very complete, and there is no shortage of delicious food with Xi'an characteristics. I have stayed in many Hyatt hotels. It is no exaggeration to say that I think the hardware of this hotel is enough to be listed on Andaz or Park Hyatt. The brand style is thoroughly displayed in this hotel. , is what I think a Hyatt hotel should be like. The hotel price is really competitive in Xi'an. Downstairs is a two-story large Tsutaya Bookstore. I bought the last remaining ymo 40-year photo album inside, which was a great surprise!
I would like to express my special thanks to Ms. Minnie from the guest service depar**ent for her attentive service. She not only called in advance to inquire about my preferences, arranged the room, prepared fresh welcome fruits for us, but also constantly cared about our various demands. Introducing the hotel's facilities and benefits made us feel like coming to Hyatt was like returning to our own home. Due to time constraints, I only stayed for one night and left in a hurry. The progressive pattern not only moves smoothly, but does not disturb each other. The room decorated with logs and auburn is warm and relaxing.

I especially like some simple but interesting small details, such as the background wall inspired by the mirage, and the wall edges and corners with the fan structure as the concept. These are enough to see the designer's intentions in the subtle places. I really like it!

Special thanks to hotel staff Jennifer Sun Jingxin for making our Grand Hyatt feel at home!
